=head1 NAME

Locale::RecodeData::CP1361

=head1 SYNOPSIS

This module is internal to libintl.  Do not use directly!

=head1 DESCRIPTION

The base for this module is generated and contains the conversion 
tables and routines for JOHAB.

JOHAB is a multi-byte encoding!


=head1 COMMENTS

The following comments have been extracted from the original charmap:

  Generated from the mappings/eastasia/johab.txt from the Unicode CDROM.

Please note that aliases listed above are not necessarily valid!

=head1 CHARACTER TABLE

The following table is sorted in the same order as the original charmap.
All character codes are in hexadecimal.  Please read 'Unicode' as
'ISO-10646-UCS4'.

        Local |  Unicode | Description
--------------+----------+----------------------------------------------
         /x00 | 00000000 | NULL (NUL)
         /x01 | 00000001 | START OF HEADING (SOH)
         /x02 | 00000002 | START OF TEXT (STX)
         /x03 | 00000003 | END OF TEXT (ETX)
         /x04 | 00000004 | END OF TRANSMISSION (EOT)
         /x05 | 00000005 | ENQUIRY (ENQ)
         /x06 | 00000006 | ACKNOWLEDGE (ACK)
         /x07 | 00000007 | BELL (BEL)
         /x08 | 00000008 | BACKSPACE (BS)
         /x09 | 00000009 | CHARACTER TABULATION (HT)
         /x0a | 0000000A | LINE FEED (LF)
         /x0b | 0000000B | LINE TABULATION (VT)
         /x0c | 0000000C | FORM FEED (FF)
         /x0d | 0000000D | CARRIAGE RETURN (CR)
         /x0e | 0000000E | SHIFT OUT (SO)
         /x0f | 0000000F | SHIFT IN (SI)
         /x10 | 00000010 | DATALINK ESCAPE (DLE)
         /x11 | 00000011 | DEVICE CONTROL ONE (DC1)
         /x12 | 00000012 | DEVICE CONTROL TWO (DC2)
